# Aetherfall base-sprite production run

Continuation of `VERTICAL_SLICE.md`, using the built-in image-generation
workflow and the locked Relicforge Miniatures / Arcane Alloy reference. Each
accepted source is chroma-keyed, extracted locally, normalized to its gameplay
canvas, and validated before its progress record is written.

## 13 — Fluxweaver

- Mix: 88% Relicforge / 12% Arcane Alloy
- Source: `sprites/source/af-013-fluxweaver-source.png`
- Final: `sprites/final/af-013-fluxweaver.png`
- Export: 128×128 RGBA

```text
Use case: stylized-concept
Asset type: final Aetherfall player-pilot vessel sprite source, stable id 13
Input images: Image 1 is the definitive blended Aetherfall production style reference. Image 2 is a composition-only orientation anchor: match its exact vertical 12-o'clock nose direction, centered vertical hull axis, three-quarter front/top game camera, and rear thruster placement at 6 o'clock. Do not copy Image 2's fire design or palette.
Primary request: Create FLUXWEAVER, form I of the water-class magitech player vessel. A compact hydrodynamic starfighter built inside a solid engineered flowing-water loop: slim pearl-and-blue teardrop hull, small aqua-glass canopy, three engraved wave chevrons, one thick oval aqueduct ring wrapping behind and in front of the hull, one bright bead at the ring tip, and one precise blue-white rear thruster. The aqueduct loop is opaque polished magical glass held in metal channels, never liquid spray. It is a piloted vessel, not humanoid or animal.
Style mix: 88% Relicforge Miniatures, 12% Arcane Alloy; premium pre-rendered 3D sprite; four to five major material zones; original design.
Style/medium: pearl ceramic, weathered silver, teal enamel, opaque cyan aqua-glass, aged brass, controlled aqua core and blue-white thruster; crisp antialiased silhouette.
Composition/framing: exactly one isolated full-body vessel, perfectly centered and vertically aligned; nose points straight upward to 12 o'clock; rear thruster points straight downward at 6 o'clock; left and right extents balanced; no diagonal hull; no sideways orientation; all ring parts visible; generous even padding; square source.
Lighting/mood: shared top-left key and cool rim; controlled glow only in canopy, ring channels, and thruster.
Scene/backdrop: perfectly flat solid #ff00ff chroma-key background, uniform with no shadow, gradient, texture, reflection, floor, vignette, border, or variation.
Constraints: no #ff00ff in subject; no cast/contact shadow, reflection, pedestal, scenery, text, logo, watermark, particles, droplets, splash, mist, foam, smoke, aura, border, frame, or transparent water; one vessel; strong 48 px silhouette.
Avoid: diagonal composition, side view, submarine, generic jet, humanoid, fish anatomy, detached water, excessive translucency, boss ornament, toy finish, vector art, pixel art, franchise resemblance.
```

## 16 — Druid

- Mix: 88% Relicforge / 12% Arcane Alloy
- Source: `sprites/source/af-016-druid-source.png`
- Final: `sprites/final/af-016-druid.png`
- Export: 128×128 RGBA

```text
Use case: stylized-concept
Asset type: final Aetherfall player-pilot vessel sprite source, stable id 16
Input images: Image 1 is the definitive blended Aetherfall production style reference. Image 2 is a composition-only orientation anchor: match its exact vertical 12-o'clock nose direction, centered vertical hull axis, three-quarter front/top game camera, and rear thruster placement at 6 o'clock. Do not copy Image 2's fire design or palette.
Primary request: Create DRUID, form I of the grass-class magic player vessel. A compact living seed-pod glider engineered as a nimble starfighter: warm brown teardrop seed-husk hull, two broad symmetrical leaf wings with central veins, small amber-green seed-glass canopy, sprouting prow with exactly two young leaves, one protected brass grass-rune collar, and one compact blue-white rear thruster integrated into root-like plating. It is a piloted living vessel with no face and no limbs.
Style mix: 88% Relicforge Miniatures, 12% Arcane Alloy; premium pre-rendered 3D sprite; four to five material zones; original bio-magitech design.
Style/medium: fibrous seed husk, matte young bark, layered green leaves, aged brass, opaque amber-green canopy glass, controlled green-gold core and blue-white thruster; crisp antialiased silhouette.
Composition/framing: exactly one isolated full-body vessel, perfectly centered and vertically aligned; pointed seed prow and two-leaf sprout face straight upward at 12 o'clock; rear thruster points straight downward at 6 o'clock; leaf wings extend evenly left and right; no diagonal hull; no sideways orientation; all tips visible; generous padding; square source.
Lighting/mood: shared top-left key and cool rim; controlled glow only in canopy, rune, and thruster.
Scene/backdrop: perfectly flat solid #ff00ff chroma-key background, uniform with no shadow, gradient, texture, reflection, floor, vignette, border, or variation.
Constraints: no #ff00ff in subject; no cast/contact shadow, reflection, pedestal, scenery, text, logo, watermark, particles, loose leaves, pollen, vines beyond hull, smoke, aura, border, or frame; one vessel; strong 48 px silhouette.
Avoid: diagonal composition, side view, animal face, humanoid, walking creature, flower mascot, giant tree, transparent leaves, boss ornament, toy finish, vector art, pixel art, franchise resemblance.
```

## 19 — Stormbinder

- Mix: 88% Relicforge / 12% Arcane Alloy
- Source: `sprites/source/af-019-stormbinder-source.png`
- Final: `sprites/final/af-019-stormbinder.png`
- Export: 128×128 RGBA

```text
Use case: stylized-concept
Asset type: final Aetherfall player-pilot vessel sprite source, stable id 19
Input images: Image 1 is the definitive blended Aetherfall production style reference. Match its Relicforge material foundation, shared three-quarter front/top game camera, top-left lighting, silhouette discipline, and restrained Arcane Alloy accents.
Primary request: Create STORMBINDER, form I of the electric-class magitech player vessel. It is a compact storm-coil interceptor: dark gunmetal teardrop hull pointed upward, two short symmetrical Tesla masts rising beside the nose with solid amber ceramic insulators and glowing yellow-white terminal spheres, a restrained hard-edged lightning motif connecting the mast housings as engraved metal and luminous enamel rather than a detached bolt, three copper coil bands around the mid-hull, a small angular storm-heart canopy, and one precise blue-white rear thruster. It must read as a piloted vessel, not a humanoid or animal. Form I is sturdy and practical.
Style mix: 88% Relicforge Miniatures, 12% Arcane Alloy. Premium pre-rendered 3D game sprite, hand-painted material variation, four to five major zones, minimal filigree, original magitech design.
Style/medium: stylized 3D vessel rendered as a clean 2D sprite; weathered gunmetal, dark ceramic, oxidized copper coils, amber insulators, opaque golden electrum glass, controlled yellow-white storm light and blue-white thruster; crisp antialiased silhouette.
Composition/framing: exactly one isolated full-body vessel centered in a square source, consistent three-quarter front/top camera, nose upward, both masts, hull, coil bands, and thruster fully visible, symmetrical silhouette, generous even padding.
Lighting/mood: shared top-left soft cinematic key and cool rim; controlled glow only in terminal spheres, storm-heart, coil seams, and thruster.
Scene/backdrop: perfectly flat solid #00ff00 chroma-key background. One uniform color only: no shadows, gradient, texture, reflection, floor, vignette, border, or lighting variation.
Constraints: never use #00ff00 in the subject; no cast shadow, contact shadow, reflection, pedestal, scenery, text, logo, watermark, particles, detached lightning, electrical aura, smoke, border, or frame; exactly one vessel; strong 48 px silhouette.
Avoid: generic fighter jet, humanoid robot, living creature, giant antennae, transparent electricity, boss ornament, excessive filigree, plastic toy finish, vector art, pixel art, existing-franchise resemblance.
```

## 14 — Tidebinder

- Mix: 76% Relicforge / 24% Arcane Alloy
- Source: `sprites/source/af-014-tidebinder-source.png`
- Final: `sprites/final/af-014-tidebinder.png`
- Export: 128×128 RGBA

```text
Use case: stylized-concept
Asset type: final Aetherfall player-pilot vessel sprite source, stable id 14
Input images: Image 1 is the definitive style reference. Image 2 is FLUXWEAVER, form I and the exact family anchor. Preserve its centered vertical pearl-and-blue hull, oval opaque aqua-glass aqueduct loop, wave-chevron grammar, aqua canopy, and single rear-thrust orientation.
Primary request: Create TIDEBINDER, form II of Fluxweaver. Evolve the compact craft into a stronger hydrodynamic vessel with a longer pearl-ceramic hull, broader teal armor shoulders, a larger faceted aqua canopy, two nested solid aqueduct channels forming one reinforced oval loop around the hull, richer engraved wave chevrons, a brass flow-regulator at the loop's lower junction, two precise blue-white rear thrusters, and small swept side fins shaped like restrained wave crests. It must unmistakably descend from Image 2, not be redesigned. The water structures are opaque polished magical glass in metal channels, never spray.
Style mix: 76% Relicforge Miniatures, 24% Arcane Alloy; premium pre-rendered 3D sprite; five to six material zones; modest engraving; original design.
Style/medium: pearl ceramic, weathered silver, teal enamel, opaque cyan aqua-glass, aged brass, controlled aqua light and blue-white thrusters; crisp antialiased silhouette.
Composition/framing: exactly one isolated vessel, identical vertical 12-o'clock nose and 6-o'clock thruster axis to Image 2, centered, symmetrical main hull, all loop channels and fins visible, no diagonal or side view, generous padding, square source.
Lighting/mood: shared top-left key and cool rim; glow only in canopy, loop channels, regulator, and thrusters.
Scene/backdrop: perfectly flat solid #ff00ff chroma-key background, uniform with no shadow, gradient, texture, reflection, floor, vignette, border, or variation.
Constraints: no #ff00ff in subject; no shadow, reflection, pedestal, scenery, text, logo, watermark, droplets, splash, mist, foam, particles, smoke, aura, border, frame, or transparent water; one vessel; readable at 48 px.
Avoid: family redesign, diagonal pose, submarine, fish anatomy, detached liquid, translucency, giant wings, boss ornament, toy finish, vector, pixel art, franchise resemblance.
```

## 17 — Grovekeeper

- Mix: 76% Relicforge / 24% Arcane Alloy
- Source: `sprites/source/af-017-grovekeeper-source.png`
- Final: `sprites/final/af-017-grovekeeper.png`

```text
Use case: stylized-concept
Asset type: final Aetherfall player-pilot vessel sprite source, stable id 17
Input images: Image 1 is the definitive style reference. Image 2 is DRUID, form I and the exact family anchor. Preserve its centered vertical seed-pod hull, fibrous bark, symmetrical leaf wings, amber-green canopy, brass grass-rune collar, two-leaf prow sprout, and blue-white rear thrust.
Primary request: Create GROVEKEEPER, form II of Druid. Evolve the seed-pod glider into a sturdier living vessel: longer layered bark-and-seed armor, broader mature leaf wings with reinforced brass vein braces, a larger faceted amber-green canopy, a protected circular grove-rune core at the chest, two additional small swept leaf stabilizers near the shoulders, a four-leaf crown sprout integrated at the nose, root-braid hull ribs, and two compact blue-white rear thrusters. It must unmistakably descend from Image 2 and remain a piloted living craft with no face or limbs.
Style mix: 76% Relicforge Miniatures, 24% Arcane Alloy; premium pre-rendered 3D sprite; five to six material zones; richer wear and engraving; original bio-magitech.
Style/medium: mature seed husk, layered bark, moss accents, green leaves, aged brass vein braces, opaque amber-green glass, controlled green-gold core and blue-white thrusters; crisp antialiased silhouette.
Composition/framing: exactly one isolated vessel, identical vertical 12-o'clock nose and 6-o'clock thruster axis to Image 2, centered, leaf wings balanced left/right, all leaf and sprout tips visible, no diagonal or side view, generous padding, square source.
Lighting/mood: shared top-left key and cool rim; glow only in canopy, grove rune, and thrusters.
Scene/backdrop: perfectly flat solid #ff00ff chroma-key background, uniform with no shadow, gradient, texture, reflection, floor, vignette, border, or variation.
Constraints: no #ff00ff in subject; no shadow, reflection, pedestal, scenery, text, logo, watermark, particles, loose leaves, pollen, vines outside hull, smoke, aura, border, or frame; one vessel; readable at 48 px.
Avoid: family redesign, diagonal pose, animal face, humanoid, walking creature, flower mascot, giant tree, transparent leaves, boss ornament, toy finish, vector, pixel art, franchise resemblance.
```

## 15 — Deepcaller

- Mix: 60% Relicforge / 40% Arcane Alloy
- Source: `sprites/source/af-015-deepcaller-source.png`
- Final: `sprites/final/af-015-deepcaller.png`
- Export: 128×128 RGBA

```text
Use case: stylized-concept
Asset type: final Aetherfall player-pilot vessel sprite source, stable id 15
Input images: Image 1 is the definitive style reference. Image 2 is TIDEBINDER, form II and the exact family anchor. Preserve its vertical pearl-and-teal hull, nested opaque aqua-glass aqueduct loop, faceted aqua canopy, wave-chevron grammar, brass flow regulator, twin thrusters, and wave-crest fins.
Primary request: Create DEEPCALLER, form III and ceremony-grade final evolution of Tidebinder. Build a majestic deep-ocean reliquary starfighter with a broader layered pearl-ceramic hull, elongated faceted abyss-blue canopy, a grand reinforced double-channel aqueduct loop around the craft, four solid radial flow vanes integrated into the ring, a large brass tidal regulator with engraved concentric wave runes, deeper navy enamel armor, four compact blue-white rear thrusters, and a restrained crown of three solid aqua-glass fins at the nose. It must unmistakably evolve from Image 2 while staying below sentinel detail density. All water-like elements are opaque engineered aqua-glass inside metal channels, never liquid spray.
Style mix: 60% Relicforge Miniatures, 40% Arcane Alloy; premium pre-rendered 3D final-form sprite; six to eight material zones; selective wear, layered engraving, sharp controlled highlights; original design.
Style/medium: pearl ceramic, navy enamel, weathered silver, polished aqua-glass, aged brass, controlled cyan/deep-blue light and blue-white thrusters; crisp antialiased silhouette.
Composition/framing: exactly one isolated vessel, identical vertical 12-o'clock nose and 6-o'clock thruster axis to Image 2, centered and balanced, all loop, vanes, fins, and thrusters visible, no diagonal or side view, generous padding, square source.
Lighting/mood: shared top-left key and cool rim with richer final-form contrast; glow only in canopy, ring channels, regulator, rune inlays, and thrusters.
Scene/backdrop: perfectly flat solid #ff00ff chroma-key background, uniform with no shadow, gradient, texture, reflection, floor, vignette, border, or variation.
Constraints: no #ff00ff in subject; no shadow, reflection, pedestal, scenery, text, logo, watermark, droplets, splash, mist, foam, particles, smoke, aura, border, frame, or transparent water; one vessel; readable at 48 px.
Avoid: family redesign, diagonal pose, submarine, fish anatomy, detached liquid, translucent spray, giant halo, boss ornament, toy finish, vector, pixel art, franchise resemblance.
```

## 22 — Drifter

- Mix: 88% Relicforge / 12% Arcane Alloy
- Source: `sprites/source/af-022-drifter-source.png`
- Final: `sprites/final/af-022-drifter.png`
- Export: 128×128 RGBA

```text
Use case: stylized-concept
Asset type: final Aetherfall player-pilot vessel sprite source, stable id 22
Input images: Image 1 is the definitive style reference. Image 2 is a composition-only anchor: match its vertical 12-o'clock nose, centered hull axis, three-quarter front/top camera, and 6-o'clock rear thruster. Do not copy its fire design.
Primary request: Create DRIFTER, form I of the normal-class magitech player vessel. It is a compact patched wanderer craft assembled from reliable salvaged parts: warm sand-colored teardrop hull, one proper weathered metal wing on the left and one visibly patched cloth-over-frame sail wing on the right, small amber lantern hanging from a short fixed prow bracket, modest honey-glass canopy, stitched leather repair plates, mismatched rivets, one tiny brass compass rune, and one blue-white rear thruster. It should feel endearing and practical, a piloted vessel with purposeful asymmetry, not junk and not a creature.
Style mix: 88% Relicforge, 12% Arcane Alloy; premium pre-rendered 3D sprite; four to five zones; minimal engraving; original design.
Style/medium: weathered cream ceramic, tan enamel, stitched sailcloth, worn leather, aged brass, dark steel, opaque honey glass, controlled lantern and thruster glow; crisp silhouette.
Composition/framing: one isolated vessel, vertical nose-up axis, centered overall mass despite intentionally mismatched wings, rear thruster down, all tips and lantern visible, no diagonal pose, generous padding, square source.
Lighting/mood: top-left key and cool rim; glow only in canopy, lantern, compass rune, and thruster.
Scene/backdrop: perfectly flat solid #00ff00 chroma-key background, fully uniform; no shadow, gradient, texture, reflection, floor, vignette, border, or variation.
Constraints: no #00ff00 in subject; no shadow, scenery, text, logo, watermark, particles, smoke, aura, border, frame, dangling loose debris, or extra craft; strong 48 px silhouette.
Avoid: sleek military jet, humanoid, animal, steampunk clutter, broken unusable craft, boss ornament, toy finish, vector, pixel art, franchise resemblance.
```

It is a compact classic sky-racer reimagined as a starfighter: slender ivory ceramic fuselage pointed upward, broad simple gull wings, restrained coral-red nose band and small circular wing markings with no letters, a solid four-blade brass propeller assembly integrated at the prow inside a narrow protective ring, small cyan open-cockpit canopy, two compact tail fins, and one blue-white rear thruster. It must read as an original piloted fantasy-tech vessel, not a real historical aircraft.
Style mix: 88% Relicforge, 12% Arcane Alloy; premium pre-rendered 3D sprite; four to five zones; minimal detail; original design.

It must read as a piloted vessel, not a living ice creature. Form I is practical and compact.

## Radiant variant generation

- Assets: all 259 `:radiant` manifest rows
- Source outputs: `sprites/source/*-radiant-source.png`
- Final outputs: `sprites/final/*-radiant.png`
- Final export sizes: 128×128 RGBA for ordinary sprites; 192×192 RGBA for sentinels, legendaries, and mythics
- Generation method: `deterministic-prismatic-palette-transform-v1`
- Builder: `tools/build-aetherfall-radiant-variants.py`
- Validation report: `manifests/radiant-validation.json`

No image-generation prompt was used for the radiant pass. The exact deterministic transformation recipe was:

```text
For each approved base sprite, preserve its complete geometry and alpha channel. Derive a stable per-asset hue rotation as 72 + (first byte of SHA-256(stableKey) modulo 64) on Pillow's 0-255 HSV hue scale, and derive the iridescent phase from the second SHA-256 byte. For colored pixels, apply the stable hue rotation, saturation = clamp(saturation * 1.12 + 10), and value = clamp(value * 1.045 + 4), blended at 82% minus a 20% neutral-material reduction. For low-saturation metal, ivory, stone, and ceramic pixels, blend 24-44% toward a luminance-preserving opal gradient oscillating between RGB 174/224/255 and RGB 255/178/228 with spatial phase sin(x * 0.073 + y * 0.051 + phase). Add a 24% pale-gold RGB 255/226/142 inner alpha rim derived from the one-pixel eroded alpha difference and a maximum 12% white lift on highlights above 68% luminance. Preserve the original alpha byte exactly for every final pixel. For high-resolution source files, estimate the chroma key from the median border color, preserve pixels within distance 14 exactly, and feather the same radiant treatment onto the subject over color-distance 14-86 in 128-row memory-safe bands. Save every final as RGBA PNG at its manifest gameplay size and validate RGBA mode, exact dimensions, transparent corners, and zero nontransparent outer-edge pixels.
```

Validation result: 259/259 radiant finals passed. The combined base-plus-radiant audit is recorded in the production handoff.

- Manifest rows: 518
- Base rows: 259
- Radiant rows: 259
- CSV rows: 518
- Progress-ledger entries: 518
- `generated-validated` entries with alpha validation: 518
- Final exports found: 518/518
- Source files found: 518/518
- 128×128 RGBA exports: 432
- 192×192 RGBA exports: 86
- Incorrect mode or dimensions: 0
- Nontransparent-corner or outer-edge failures: 0
- Radiant validation report: 259/259 passed
